<script type="text/JavaScript">

$("input[name*='g']").inputmask({
"mask": "###########",
 "numericInput": true,
    "definitions": {
        '#': { validator: "[0-9]", cardinality: 1 }
    },

});
	function getParameterByName(name, url) {
		if (!url) url = window.location.href;
		name = name.replace(/[\[\]]/g, "\\$&");
		var regex = new RegExp("[?&]" + name + "(=([^&#]*)|&|#|$)"),
			results = regex.exec(url);
		if (!results) return '';
		if (!results[2]) return '';
		return decodeURIComponent(results[2].replace(/\+/g, " "));
	}
	
	var finger = getParameterByName('f');
	document.getElementById('yt1').value = finger;
	
	
</script>

[% Begin Unverified Perl
use Digest::SHA qw(hmac_sha256_base64);

my $g = GETVALUE("g");
my $s = GETVALUE("s");
my $c = GETVALUE("c");
my $x = "1";
my $x2 = "713";

#return  $g."|".$s."|".$c."|".$x."|".$x2;

my $digest = hmac_sha256_base64($g."|".$s."|".$c."|".$x."|".$x2, "SiaInsight/(!+A3");
#$digest =~ s/\+/\%2B/; 
#$digest =~ s/\+/\%2B/g;

#my $str = 'so0y0omQfzfIX%2BAXEHU1+2ZpBQ7lPuqz3+qM06V5xds===';
#$url_text =~ s/([^;\/?:@&=+\$,A-Za-z0-9\-_.!~*'()])/sprintf( "%%%02X",+ ord( $1 ) )/ge;
$digest =~ s/([^\$A-Za-z0-9\-_.~])/sprintf( "%%%02X",+ ord( $1 ) )/ge;
  
# digest is currently: qnR8UCqJggD55PohusaBNviGoOJ67HC6Btry4qXLVZc

# Fix padding of Base64 digests
while (length($digest) % 4) {
    $digest .= '=';
}

#return $digest;
# digest is now: qnR8UCqJggD55PohusaBNviGoOJ67HC6Btry4qXLVZc=

SETVALUE("x2", $digest);

$digest = hmac_sha256_base64($g."|".$s."|".$c."|2|".$x2, "SiaInsight/(!+A3");
$digest =~ s/([^\$A-Za-z0-9\-_.~])/sprintf( "%%%02X",+ ord( $1 ) )/ge;
while (length($digest) % 4) {
    $digest .= '=';
}
SETVALUE("x2s", $digest);

function Trimle(strValue) {
    var objRegExp, Flag;

    Flag = true;
    if(objRegExp.test(strValue))
        {
               strValue = strValue.replace(objRegExp, '');

[JavaScript Verification]:

    var ANKETORKOD = document.mainform['SahaBilgi_ANKETORKOD'].value;
    var GsmExp = /^(?!0)[0-9]{10}?$/;
    var PhoneExp = /^(212|216)(?!0)[0-9]{7}?$/;
				
    if (CepTel.length > 0 && GsmExp.test(CepTel) == false)
        {

            document.mainform['SahaBilgi_ANKETORKOD'].focus();
		}

<input name="[% QuestionName() %]_Latitude" id="[% QuestionName() %]_Latitude" type="hidden" value="">
<input name="[% QuestionName() %]_Longitude" id="[% QuestionName() %]_Longitude" type="hidden" value="">
<input name="[% QuestionName() %]_Accuracy" id="[% QuestionName() %]_Accuracy" type="hidden" value="">
<input name="[% QuestionName() %]_Error" id="[% QuestionName() %]_Error" type="hidden" value="">

<script>
$(document).ready(function(){
	navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(function(pos){
		$('#[% QuestionName() %]_Latitude').val(pos.coords.latitude);
		$('#[% QuestionName() %]_Longitude').val(pos.coords.longitude);
		$('#[% QuestionName() %]_Accuracy').val(pos.coords.accuracy);
	}, function(err){
		$('#[% QuestionName() %]_Error').val('Err #' + err.code + ': ' + err.message);
	}, {
		enableHighAccuracy: true,
		timeout: 10000,
		maximumAge: 0
	});
})
</script>

[Footer]:
<script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
        function disableNavgs() {
            if (document.getElementById("next_button") != null)
                document.getElementById("next_button").style.visibility = 'hidden';
        }

        function enableNavgs() {
            if (document.getElementById("next_button") != null)
                document.getElementById("next_button").style.visibility = 'visible';
        }

        function doWork() {
            disableNavgs(); 
            setTimeout(enableNavgs, 10000);
        }

        window.onload = doWork
    </script>

Logic: 

Begin Unverified Perl
my $list=LISTLENGTH("GRUPYASList");
for (my $i=1; $i<=$list; $i++)
{
	my @arr=split(/-/,LISTLABEL("GRUPYASList",$i));
    if (@arr[1]!="")
    {
		for (my $age=@arr[0]; $age<=@arr[1]; $age++)
		{
			if (VALUE("ACIKYAS")==$age)
			{
				ADD("GRUPYASList",$i);
				last;
			}
		}
 	}
	if (TEXTEXISTS(@arr[0],"+") && MID(@arr[0],1,2) < VALUE("ACIKYAS") )
	{
		ADD("GRUPYASList",$i);	
		last;
	}
		
}
	
End Unverified

<input name="[% QuestionName() %]_Latitude" id="[% QuestionName() %]_Latitude" type="hidden" value="">
<input name="[% QuestionName() %]_Longitude" id="[% QuestionName() %]_Longitude" type="hidden" value="">
<input name="[% QuestionName() %]_Accuracy" id="[% QuestionName() %]_Accuracy" type="hidden" value="">

<script>
$(document).ready(function(){
	navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(function(pos){
		$('#[% QuestionName() %]_Latitude').val(pos.coords.latitude);
		$('#[% QuestionName() %]_Longitude').val(pos.coords.longitude);
		$('#[% QuestionName() %]_Accuracy').val(pos.coords.accuracy);
	}, function(err){
		$('#[% QuestionName() %]_Error').val('Err #' + err.code + ': ' + err.message);
	}, {
		enableHighAccuracy: true,
		timeout: 10000,
		maximumAge: 0
	});
})
</script>

[Footer]:
<script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
        function disableNavgs() {
            if (document.getElementById("next_button") != null)
                document.getElementById("next_button").style.visibility = 'hidden';
        }

        function enableNavgs() {
            if (document.getElementById("next_button") != null)
                document.getElementById("next_button").style.visibility = 'visible';
        }

        function doWork() {
            disableNavgs(); 
            setTimeout(enableNavgs, 10000);
        }

        window.onload = doWork
    </script>

===========================
List Name: GRUPYASList
===========================
Type: Predefined
Number of Items: 4
---------------------------

1	15-17
2	18-24
3	25-35
4	36-45

===========================
List Name: GrupYasCons
===========================
Type: Constructed
Parent List: GRUPYASList
---------------------------

[Logic]:
Begin Unverified Perl
my $list=LISTLENGTH("GRUPYASList");
for (my $i=1; $i<=$list; $i++)
{
	my @arr=split(/-/,LISTLABEL("GRUPYASList",$i));
    if (@arr[1]!="")
    {
		for (my $age=@arr[0]; $age<=@arr[1]; $age++)
		{
			if (VALUE("ACIKYAS")==$age)
			{
				ADD("GRUPYASList",$i);
				last;
			}
		}
 	}
	if (TEXTEXISTS(@arr[0],"+") && MID(@arr[0],1,2) < VALUE("ACIKYAS") )
	{
		ADD("GRUPYASList",$i);	
		last;
	}
		
}
	
End Unverified

function hissiz(text) {
text = text.replace(/ğ/g, "g");
text = text.replace(/Ğ/g, "G");
text = text.replace(/ü/g, "u");
text = text.replace(/Ü/g, "U");
text = text.replace(/ş/g, "s");
text = text.replace(/Ş/g, "S");
text = text.replace(/İ/g, "I");
text = text.replace(/ı/g, "i");
text = text.replace(/ö/g, "o");
text = text.replace(/Ö/g, "O");
text = text.replace(/ç/g, "c");
text = text.replace(/Ç/g, "C");
return text;
}
</script> -->

[Out of Range (Numeric)]:

[Invalid Input (Numeric)]:
Lütfen numerik giriş yapınız. [%ErrText()%]

[Minimum Characters]:
Minumum [%ErrMin()%] karakter girmelisiniz.  [%ErrText()%]

[Maximum Characters]:
Maksimum [%ErrMax()%] karakter giriş yapabilirsiniz.  [%ErrText()%]

[Password Closed]:
Ankete yalnızca bir kez katılma hakkı bulunmaktadır.Teşekkürler.

[Finished]:
Bu anket daha önce tarafınızdan doldurulmuştur.Değerli zamanınız için teşekkürler.

[Invalid Login]:
Giriş onaylanmadı. Erişim engellendi.

[Rank]:

[Rank Count]:

[None of the Above]:
Bu seçeneği, diğer seçenekler ile beraber kullanamazsınız.  [%ErrText()%]

[Constant Sum]:
Cevapların toplamı [%ErrTotal()%] olmalıdır.[%ErrText()%]

[MaxDiff Unique Answers]:
Aynı ürün birden fazla kez seçilemez. [%ErrText()%]

[ACBC Prohibited]:
You've chosen some features that together are not feasible. The prohibited combinations are highlighted. Please reconsider.  [%ErrText()%]

[ACBC Price Adjustment Warning]:
The price has changed on one or more of the items that you selected. Please review the price.

[Survey Paused]:

Ürün için iyi ve kötü ifadesi beraber seçilemez.
